<div class="entry-content single-content">
	
<h1 class="wp-block-heading">Bhoomi Online RTC Login, Pahani Mutation Mojini Land Records</h1>



<p>The <a href="https://bhoomi-rtconline.com/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Bhoomi Online</a> RTC Portal, launched by the Karnataka government, provides citizens with easy access to land records, including RTC (Pahani), Mutation, Khata Extract, and Revenue Maps. By digitizing key documents, the portal ensures transparency, reduces legal conflicts, and simplifies land management. </p>



<p>It offers services like mutation status checks, land conversion applications, and digitally signed records, along with tools like i-Wallet and RTC Sketch for secure management. This paperless initiative benefits landowners, farmers, and government institutions by providing quick, accurate online access to land details.</p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_096c30-6d alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-3-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_3944e5-52 kb-section-has-overlay"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-advancedbtn kb-buttons-wrap kb-btns10_d34dec-10"><a class="kb-button kt-button button kb-btn10_f55fdd-9e kt-btn-size-standard kt-btn-width-type-auto kb-btn-global-fill  kt-btn-has-text-true kt-btn-has-svg-false  wp-block-kadence-singlebtn" href="https://landrecords.karnataka.gov.in/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow"><span class="kt-btn-inner-text">Bhoomi Online</span></a></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_337944-98 kb-section-has-overlay"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-advancedbtn kb-buttons-wrap kb-btns10_a1a140-e1"><a class="kb-button kt-button button kb-btn10_fc1ac0-ea kt-btn-size-standard kt-btn-width-type-auto kb-btn-global-fill  kt-btn-has-text-true kt-btn-has-svg-false  wp-block-kadence-singlebtn" href="https://landrecords.karnataka.gov.in/Service2/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow"><span class="kt-btn-inner-text">View RTC (Pahani)</span></a></div>
</div></div>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-theme-palette-9-color has-theme-palette-3-background-color has-text-color has-background has-link-color has-medium-font-size wp-elements-78d5d226fbb6c900779bad4875d84e15" style="border-top-left-radius:30px;border-bottom-right-radius:30px">Bhoomi RTC: Simplifying Land Records in Karnataka</h2>



<p>Bhoomi RTC is a digital document that contains crucial details about land ownership, tenancy, cultivation, and crops, serving legal purposes like transactions, loans, and disputes. Launched in 2000 by the Karnataka government, the Bhoomi portal digitizes these records, making them accessible online and eliminating the need for citizens to visit revenue offices, thus reducing delays.</p>



<p>The Bhoomi RTC platform covers 175 taluks and 6,000 gram panchayats, providing services such as land status checks, mutation applications, and access to land records. It enhances transparency in land transactions, minimizes fraud, and supports the resolution of land-related conflicts, streamlining the process and making it more efficient and accessible for all.</p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-theme-palette-9-color has-theme-palette-3-background-color has-text-color has-background has-link-color has-medium-font-size wp-elements-a30c8f1a6ac5c49fd315d018de420b4a" style="border-top-left-radius:30px;border-bottom-right-radius:30px">Land Services Available on Bhoomi Online</h2>

<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-10_1cbf4c-f7"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Access the Crop Loan Waiver system and land management services.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p><strong>Other Features:</strong></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items10_439296-57 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-10_daae8d-60"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">View and track new taluks.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-10_33ee79-35"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Access tools like name matching algorithms and Dishaank services.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-10_870e64-a8"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Convert binary files from ISFOC to Unicode for easier document processing.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p><strong>User-Friendly Interface:</strong></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items10_f7f16f-94 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-10_974472-6b"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Easy-to-navigate dashboard for managing all services and land-related documents.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-theme-palette-9-color has-theme-palette-3-background-color has-text-color has-background has-link-color has-medium-font-size wp-elements-65c972afaedeeaa22d4bcdd912e5cf30" style="border-top-left-radius:30px;border-bottom-right-radius:30px">What is Bhoomi Online Portal?</h2>



<p>&nbsp;The Bhoomi Online Portal offers a comprehensive platform for citizens of Karnataka to access and manage land records efficiently. This portal provides essential services such as viewing RTC (Pahani), checking mutation reports, and accessing revenue maps. It also includes services like land conversion applications and survey number checks through the KSLIS portal, enabling users to manage their land-related tasks without the need for physical visits to government offices.</p>



<p>The portal also supports i-RTC Wallet, allowing users to manage payments for land record services securely. Additionally, Bhoomi provides access to various reports and documents, including Khata Extracts, dispute case tracking, and affidavit-based land conversion status. This digital platform enhances transparency and simplifies the process of obtaining critical land information.</p>



<p>With over 20 million records available, Bhoomi plays a key role in modernizing land administration in Karnataka, making land records more accessible and reducing errors associated with manual record-keeping. The portal&#8217;s user-friendly interface ensures that even those unfamiliar with technology can navigate it effectively.</p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-theme-palette-9-color has-theme-palette-3-background-color has-text-color has-background has-link-color has-medium-font-size wp-elements-ff5134555b868ca9b68ff32d4549631f" style="border-top-left-radius:30px;border-bottom-right-radius:30px">Steps to Check RTC (Pahani) on Bhoomi Online Portal</h2>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_62ab1d-88 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-3-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_32e051-93" data-aos="slide-left" data-aos-duration="950"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_96671d-c6 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_69e022-4b"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p class="kt-adv-heading10_419f45-e2 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading kt-adv-heading-has-icon" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading10_419f45-e2"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-adv-heading-icon kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kb-adv-heading-icon-side-left"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kb-adv-text-inner"><strong><strong><strong>Visit the Bhoomi Portal</strong>: </strong></strong></span></p></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_7e4af7-68"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p>Open your browser and navigate to the official Bhoomi website,<a href="https://landrecords.karnataka.gov.in" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow">landrecords.karnataka.gov.in</a>.</p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_21cc4e-ed" data-aos="slide-left" data-aos-duration="950"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_448edf-7a alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_119c34-9f"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p class="kt-adv-heading10_91e99d-8d wp-block-kadence-advancedheading kt-adv-heading-has-icon" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading10_91e99d-8d"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-adv-heading-icon kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kb-adv-heading-icon-side-left"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kb-adv-text-inner"><strong><strong><strong>Select ‘RTC/Pahani’</strong>: </strong></strong></span></p></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_b9c0e9-31"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p>On the homepage, locate and click on the option related to RTC (Pahani).</p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_22bffb-e0" data-aos="slide-left" data-aos-duration="950"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_7cf61f-c2 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_2b47b4-a8"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p class="kt-adv-heading10_9dc782-70 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading kt-adv-heading-has-icon" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading10_9dc782-70"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-adv-heading-icon kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kb-adv-heading-icon-side-left"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kb-adv-text-inner"><strong><strong><strong><strong>Select Your District</strong>: </strong></strong></strong></span></p></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_ab86ab-4a"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p>A dropdown menu will appear, allowing you to select your district.</p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_04e1fe-d5" data-aos="slide-right" data-aos-duration="950"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_461a73-d5 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_1be6db-a0"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p class="kt-adv-heading10_c680f3-40 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading kt-adv-heading-has-icon" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading10_c680f3-40"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-adv-heading-icon kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kb-adv-heading-icon-side-left"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kb-adv-text-inner"><strong><strong><strong>Select the Taluk</strong>: </strong></strong></span></p></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_43a178-0a"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p>After selecting the district, choose the Taluk where your land is located.</p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_bbb5f9-2d" data-aos="slide-right" data-aos-duration="950"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_f97db6-b2 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_37f3e4-c0"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p class="kt-adv-heading10_663515-0c wp-block-kadence-advancedheading kt-adv-heading-has-icon" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading10_663515-0c"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-adv-heading-icon kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kb-adv-heading-icon-side-left"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kb-adv-text-inner"><strong><strong><strong>Choose the Hobli</strong>: </strong></strong></span></p></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_7887a5-c3"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p>Next, select the Hobli (sub-division of the Taluk) corresponding to your land.</p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_302c28-02" data-aos="slide-right" data-aos-duration="950"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_1d4902-63 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_55f56f-f2"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p class="kt-adv-heading10_a8155e-a2 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading kt-adv-heading-has-icon" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading10_a8155e-a2"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-adv-heading-icon kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kb-adv-heading-icon-side-left"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kb-adv-text-inner"><strong><strong><strong>Enter the Survey Number</strong>: </strong></strong></span></p></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_1d593e-37"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p>Provide the survey number of your land. This is crucial for locating the exact land record.</p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_c4dbd8-4c alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-3-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_92008e-f3" data-aos="slide-left" data-aos-duration="950"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_bcf30c-b1 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_048013-c0"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p class="kt-adv-heading10_6d28ce-9d wp-block-kadence-advancedheading kt-adv-heading-has-icon" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading10_6d28ce-9d"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-adv-heading-icon kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kb-adv-heading-icon-side-left"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kb-adv-text-inner"><strong><strong><strong>Submit the Information</strong>: </strong></strong></span></p></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_4c7f1d-84"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p>Click the ‘Submit’ button after entering the required details.</p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_11064d-97" data-aos="slide-right" data-aos-duration="950"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_c7f669-31 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_d873d3-6d"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p class="kt-adv-heading10_800697-23 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading kt-adv-heading-has-icon" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading10_800697-23"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-adv-heading-icon kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kb-adv-heading-icon-side-left"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kb-adv-text-inner"><strong><strong><strong>View the RTC</strong>: </strong></strong></span></p></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_cdc8fc-30"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p>Your RTC document will appear on the screen. You can review the details and download or print them for your records.</p>
</div></div>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-theme-palette-9-color has-theme-palette-3-background-color has-text-color has-background has-link-color has-medium-font-size wp-elements-9ff6f77147e1f05ecd5168c5abf7310b" style="border-top-left-radius:30px;border-bottom-right-radius:30px"><strong><strong>Purpose of the Bhoomi RTC Online Portal</strong></strong></h2>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_e6ec22-93 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_6cd749-41"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_6bff66-88"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">1</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text">The Bhoomi RTC Online Portal was launched in 2000 by the Karnataka government to digitize land records, replacing the traditional paper-based system.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_bde317-f2"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_b71954-0b"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">2</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text">It provides easy online access to land information, improving transparency, efficiency, and accessibility.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_c6a810-3c"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_549f47-36"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">3</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text">Over 20 million land records have been digitized, streamlining land administration and reducing the need for in-person visits.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_1ca58b-f3"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_1d0a63-95"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">4</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text">The portal promotes clarity, helps resolve land disputes, enhances agricultural lending, and fosters confidence among landowners and investors.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-theme-palette-9-color has-theme-palette-3-background-color has-text-color has-background has-link-color has-medium-font-size wp-elements-5c496c21d42b6a8575bba19d1c6a32eb" style="border-top-left-radius:30px;border-bottom-right-radius:30px">Key Features of the Bhoomi RTC Portal</h2>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_5b8e04-27 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_6834f4-71"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_8ccd01-c4"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">1</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>RTC (Record of Rights, Tenancy, and Crops) – Also Known as Pahani<br></strong>The Bhoomi RTC portal provides access to essential land documents, such as the RTC (Pahani). The RTC contains key details including the owner&#8217;s name, survey number, land type and usage, tenancy information, and crop details. This document is crucial for legal processes like ownership verification, loan applications, and dispute resolution. Users can download the RTC online, avoiding the need for in-person visits to government offices.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_966f2c-12"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_986c8a-58"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">2</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>Mutation Services<br></strong> Mutation is the process of updating land records when ownership changes, such as through sale or inheritance. The Bhoomi portal allows users to check the status of mutation online, making the process more efficient and reducing the need for paperwork. This service simplifies the update process and ensures that land records remain current.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_317869-28"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_81c0ce-bb"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">3</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>Other Services Provided:</strong> The portal offers various services, such as:<br>Viewing RTC/Pahani documents<br>Accessing Khata extracts<br>Tracking mutation status<br>Viewing revenue maps<br>Requesting survey documents and accessing survey documentation<br><br>These services provide citizens with a comprehensive solution for land-related needs, all available through a user-friendly interface designed to be accessible even to users with limited digital skills.<br></p></div></span></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_b4c517-ce"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_5b1cb3-2d"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">4</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>Impact and Reach<br></strong>Bhoomi has significantly modernized the land record system in Karnataka, facilitating faster resolutions, reducing corruption, and improving governance. By allowing citizens to independently verify ownership records, the portal fosters accountability and reduces legal conflicts. Bhoomi has set an example for other states, inspiring similar initiatives like Patta Chitta in Tamil Nadu and Meebhoomi in Andhra Pradesh. <a href="https://pattachita.com/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Patta Chitta</a>, linked to Aadhaar, is crucial for property transactions, dispute resolution, and ownership verification.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_1cff8b-a5 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_e1c074-5f"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_f10d5c-be"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">5</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>Easy Access to Land Records</strong>: The portal provides easy online access to land records 24/7, eliminating the need for physical visits to government offices.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_998dc6-3d"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_2b01fc-46"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">6</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>Search Facility</strong>: Users can search for records by entering survey number, property owner name, and other relevant details. This saves time for both landowners and buyers.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_7a918d-64"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_0537bd-e6"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">7</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>Revenue and Ownership Information</strong>: The portal offers detailed records of land revenue, ownership, land classification, and crop information, which are essential for legal and agricultural purposes.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_7df561-9a"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_c20570-56"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">8</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>Transparency and Trust</strong>: The portal reduces corruption and promotes transparency by minimizing human interference in the land records process.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_edb6dd-0d alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_5fd010-31"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_b8654e-55"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">9</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>Simplification of Land Transactions</strong>: Bhoomi simplifies land transactions by allowing users to verify land records before buying or selling property, ensuring legitimacy and preventing fraud.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_2c7314-91"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_b8c2af-3b"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">10</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>Mobile-Friendly</strong>: The portal is accessible on mobile devices, providing users with convenient access to land records on the go.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>

</div></div>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-theme-palette-9-color has-theme-palette-3-background-color has-text-color has-background has-link-color has-medium-font-size wp-elements-f06e14c68b8824fc9b7b7e6846f7e3a8" style="border-top-left-radius:30px;border-bottom-right-radius:30px">How to Register on the Bhoomi Portal</h2>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">Why Register on the Bhoomi Portal?</h3>



<p><strong><br></strong>Registering on the Bhoomi portal allows you to access land record details and various land-related services, including RTC (Record of Rights, Tenancy, and Crops), revenue maps, and more. Without registration, you will not be able to avail yourself of these essential services.</p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">Steps to Register a New Account</h3>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_ef4187-0f alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_08be23-02"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_594d1e-67"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">1</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>Visit the Official Website</strong>: Go to the Bhoomi portal&#8217;s official login page: <a href="https://landrecords.karnataka.gov.in/service78/Login.aspx" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Bhoomi Portal Login</a>.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_7b4a41-c8"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_aa4fc7-00"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">2</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>Click &#8216;Create Account&#8217;</strong>: Once on the login page, click the “Create Account” button to begin the registration process.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_5f710d-9c"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_251056-97"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">3</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>Enter Required Details</strong>: Fill in the form with your first name, last name, Aadhaar number, email address, mobile number, and address.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_cfd94d-3d"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_e59c14-2d"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">4</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>Verify Mobile Number</strong>: You will receive an OTP (One-Time Password) on your mobile number. Enter this OTP correctly to verify your mobile number.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_233418-c9 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_08ac41-82"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_c51ec1-b2"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">5</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>Submit the Form</strong>: After entering all the required details and verifying your mobile number, click the “Sign Up/Submit” button to complete the registration process.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_b6827d-ef"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"></div></div>

</div></div>


<h3 class="wp-block-heading">Creating a New Account (If You Don&#8217;t Have One)</h3>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_1b9755-5f alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_d12807-ba"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_e73755-11"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">1</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>Click &#8216;Register&#8217;</strong>: On the login page, find and click the “Register” or “Create Account” option to start the registration process.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_0ee641-56"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_391d83-40"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">2</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>Provide Required Information</strong>: You will need to enter:<br>Mobile Number<br>District, Taluk, Village (where your land is located)<br>Survey Number (unique property identifier)<br>Password (create a strong password)</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_407f45-6d"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_e6be1b-80"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">3</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>Submit the Information</strong>: After entering all necessary details, click “Submit” to create your account.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_406ae4-b5"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_f442eb-73"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">4</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>Confirmation</strong>: Upon successful registration, you will receive a confirmation message or SMS on your mobile number.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<h4 class="wp-block-heading has-theme-palette-1-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-ef8e538733cb8bdab7b5762e7976d2d8">Login with Existing Account</h4>



<p><strong><br></strong>If you already have an account, simply visit the Bhoomi portal’s login page and enter your credentials to access the services.</p>



<ol class="wp-block-list">
<li></li>
</ol>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-theme-palette-9-color has-theme-palette-3-background-color has-text-color has-background has-link-color has-medium-font-size wp-elements-c8b44c89252a2a3707a3998d1b203cd2" style="border-top-left-radius:30px;border-bottom-right-radius:30px">Bhoomi Online RTC Login Process</h2>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_e6ac71-f4 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_89b455-aa"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_2ab494-47"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">1</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>Open the Official Website<br></strong> Open any browser (Google Chrome, Mozilla Firefox, etc.) and visit the official Bhoomi Online RTC website: <a href="https://landrecords.karnataka.gov.in/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow">Bhoomi Portal</a>.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_2cefd9-9d"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_a9d3bf-aa"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">2</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>Locate the Login Section<br></strong>On the homepage, find the login section, usually located at the top or center of the page.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_be1cbe-53"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_b274f5-19"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">3</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong><strong>Enter Your Login Credentials<br></strong>User ID</strong>: Enter your unique User ID assigned to you during registration.<br><strong>Password</strong>: Enter the password associated with your account.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_120a72-d1"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box10_1d8585-b9"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-left"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-container kt-info-number-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-number-inner-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-number">4</div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><strong>Complete Captcha Verification</strong> <strong>&amp; <strong>Click Login</strong><br></strong> To ensure security, you will be prompted to solve a CAPTCHA. Enter the characters displayed in the captcha box correctly.  After entering your login credentials and captcha correctly, click on the “Login” button to access your Bhoomi Online portal.</p></div></span></div>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-theme-palette-9-color has-theme-palette-3-background-color has-text-color has-background has-link-color has-medium-font-size wp-elements-5f8b8179497b1556dcb9b5361b549d07" style="border-top-left-radius:30px;border-bottom-right-radius:30px">How to Extract a Mutation Report on the Bhoomi Online Portal</h2>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_5cfc31-59 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-3-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_557f36-41"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p><strong>Access the Bhoomi Portal<br></strong>Visit the Bhoomi website at <a href="https://landrecords.karnataka.gov.in/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow">Bhoomi Online Portal</a>.<br></p>



<p>Locate the option for viewing RTC and Mutation Reports (MR) on the homepage. Click on it to proceed.</p>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_095baf-04"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p class="kt-adv-heading10_3209db-19 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading10_3209db-19"><strong>Select Mutation Option<br></strong>On the next page, look for the mutation option.<br><br>Enter the required details, such as <strong>District</strong>, <strong>Taluk</strong>, <strong>Hobli</strong>, <strong>Village</strong>, and <strong>Survey Number</strong>.</p>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_d1ae1f-eb"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p class="kt-adv-heading10_414d04-b8 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading10_414d04-b8"><strong>Fetch Mutation Details<br></strong>The mutation-related information will be displayed. To view the specifics, select the <strong>Preview</strong> option.<br>After entering all the necessary information, click the <strong>Fetch Details</strong> button.</p>
</div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_5b6472-42 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-3-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_f424f8-fe"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p><strong>Download/Save the Report<br></strong>After viewing the mutation details, you can save the report for future reference or print a hard copy for your records.</p>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_966e43-6f"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_6de28c-9a"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"></div></div>

</div></div>


<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-theme-palette-9-color has-theme-palette-3-background-color has-text-color has-background has-link-color has-medium-font-size wp-elements-220055203ddfa1d8494ccbd30e23df0e" style="border-top-left-radius:30px;border-bottom-right-radius:30px">Steps to Check Mutation Status on Bhoomi Online Portal</h2>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_809b64-26 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-3-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_af7885-15" data-aos="slide-left" data-aos-duration="950"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_7abddf-c5 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_a8866d-3c"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p class="kt-adv-heading10_090700-1d wp-block-kadence-advancedheading kt-adv-heading-has-icon" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading10_090700-1d"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-adv-heading-icon kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kb-adv-heading-icon-side-left"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kb-adv-text-inner"><strong><strong><strong>Visit the Bhoomi Portal</strong></strong></strong></span></p></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_4af4dd-d7"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p> Open your web browser and navigate to the official Bhoomi website: <a href="https://landrecords.karnataka.gov.in/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Bhoomi Portal</a>.<br></p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_7a5e7f-bc" data-aos="slide-left" data-aos-duration="950"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_555de0-da alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_8a0f61-ed"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p class="kt-adv-heading10_15d6ce-dc wp-block-kadence-advancedheading kt-adv-heading-has-icon" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading10_15d6ce-dc"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-adv-heading-icon kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kb-adv-heading-icon-side-left"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kb-adv-text-inner"><strong><strong><strong>Select ‘Check Mutation Status’</strong></strong></strong></span></p></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_94f7bd-11"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p> On the homepage, look for the option labeled “Check Mutation Status” or a similar link and click on it.<br></p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_ede80a-9d" data-aos="slide-left" data-aos-duration="950"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_b1baf6-c2 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_c3b460-8d"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p class="kt-adv-heading10_074db9-31 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading kt-adv-heading-has-icon" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading10_074db9-31"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-adv-heading-icon kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kb-adv-heading-icon-side-left"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kb-adv-text-inner"><strong><strong><strong><strong>Enter Required Details</strong></strong></strong></strong></span></p></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_f54b4f-93"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p> Fill in the necessary information, such as the <strong>District</strong>, <strong>Taluk</strong>, <strong>Hobli</strong>, and <strong>Survey Number</strong> or <strong>Application Number</strong>.<br></p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_1cd87d-cf" data-aos="slide-right" data-aos-duration="950"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_eb8a7c-e9 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_c0daa6-db"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p class="kt-adv-heading10_d3e6fb-25 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading kt-adv-heading-has-icon" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading10_d3e6fb-25"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-adv-heading-icon kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kb-adv-heading-icon-side-left"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kb-adv-text-inner"><strong><strong><strong>Submit the Information</strong></strong></strong></span></p></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_823a95-11"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p> After entering the details, click the <strong>Submit</strong> button to proceed.<br></p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_fced68-b5" data-aos="slide-right" data-aos-duration="950"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_a51a70-5f alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_f806f7-c0"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p class="kt-adv-heading10_56905b-d5 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading kt-adv-heading-has-icon" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading10_56905b-d5"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-adv-heading-icon kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kb-adv-heading-icon-side-left"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kb-adv-text-inner"><strong><strong><strong>View Status</strong></strong></strong></span></p></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_300245-a9"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">

</div></div>

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_73910f-ab"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">

<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-theme-palette-9-color has-theme-palette-3-background-color has-text-color has-background has-link-color has-medium-font-size wp-elements-1b376a05a288eec962d0a6da9154bcc1" style="border-top-left-radius:30px;border-bottom-right-radius:30px">How to Check Affidavit-Based Land Conversion Status in Karnataka</h2>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_8f9b5a-e0 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-3-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_7868b5-49" data-aos="slide-left" data-aos-duration="950"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_142cde-f9 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_516406-ed"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p class="kt-adv-heading10_23f7ba-5d wp-block-kadence-advancedheading kt-adv-heading-has-icon" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading10_23f7ba-5d"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-adv-heading-icon kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kb-adv-heading-icon-side-left"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kb-adv-text-inner"><strong><strong><strong>Visit the Official Website</strong></strong></strong></span></p></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_63524d-47"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p>Open your browser and go to the official land conversion website: <a href="https://landconversion.karnataka.gov.in/Service74/afdlcreport/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow">Land Conversion Status</a>.<br></p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_1e663d-a8" data-aos="slide-left" data-aos-duration="950"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_d05136-77 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_73e283-a5"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p class="kt-adv-heading10_01d7cc-13 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading kt-adv-heading-has-icon" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading10_01d7cc-13"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-adv-heading-icon kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kb-adv-heading-icon-side-left"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kb-adv-text-inner"><strong><strong><strong>Choose a Report Option</strong></strong></strong></span></p></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_da7fd6-2f"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p>On the page, you will find several options to view the land conversion status, including:</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>Pendency with RD User</li>



<li>Pendency Report with Request ID</li>



<li>Pendency with Other Departments</li>



<li>Pendency of UPOR Report</li>



<li>Disposed Request</li>



<li>Select the option that best matches your need.</li>
</ul>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_1dafd3-59" data-aos="slide-left" data-aos-duration="950"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_9411da-6d alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_bbbfe8-c1"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p class="kt-adv-heading10_14e313-8f wp-block-kadence-advancedheading kt-adv-heading-has-icon" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading10_14e313-8f"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-adv-heading-icon kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kb-adv-heading-icon-side-left"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kb-adv-text-inner"><strong><strong><strong><strong>Enter Required Details</strong></strong></strong></strong></span></p></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_9d0603-22"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p>After selecting the relevant report type, enter your <strong>District</strong> in the provided field.<br></p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_60e1c1-f1" data-aos="slide-right" data-aos-duration="950"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_f1da0c-ee alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_c1cd60-0f"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p class="kt-adv-heading10_44cfbb-cb wp-block-kadence-advancedheading kt-adv-heading-has-icon" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading10_44cfbb-cb"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-adv-heading-icon kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kb-adv-heading-icon-side-left"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kb-adv-text-inner"><strong><strong><strong>Fetch the Report</strong></strong></strong></span></p></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_6c1b73-39"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p>Click the <strong>“Fetch Report”</strong> button. The system will retrieve and display the relevant data based on the information you’ve entered.</p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_7038b5-85" data-aos="slide-right" data-aos-duration="950"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_352f61-01 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_30e952-49"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p class="kt-adv-heading10_609f50-c0 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading kt-adv-heading-has-icon" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading10_609f50-c0"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-adv-heading-icon kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kb-adv-heading-icon-side-left"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span><span class="kb-adv-text-inner"><strong><strong><strong>View Status</strong></strong></strong></span></p></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_4d97b4-b3"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p>Once the data is loaded, you can view detailed information regarding your affidavit-based land conversion request, including the current status, any pending departments, and actions taken.</p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-theme-palette-9-color has-theme-palette-3-background-color has-text-color has-background has-link-color has-medium-font-size wp-elements-10b9d367199dc00565ba605b9032d613" style="border-top-left-radius:30px;border-bottom-right-radius:30px">How to Check Survey Number in Karnataka</h2>



<p>A Survey Number is a unique identifier assigned to a specific land parcel. To check the survey number of your land in Karnataka, you can use the Karnataka State Land Information System (KSLIS) or the Bhoomi Online portal.</p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">Steps to Check Survey Number:</h3>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_e7c3f6-f0 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-3-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column10_a05666-62" data-aos="slide-left" data-aos-duration="950"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id10_801969-14 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-theme-palette-9-color has-theme-palette-3-background-color has-text-color has-background has-link-color has-medium-font-size wp-elements-a20a7d7566c83243ee221b9a59d13cf0" style="border-top-left-radius:30px;border-bottom-right-radius:30px">How to Request Survey Documents Online</h2>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items10_6ca49e-3b kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-10_669d98-9a"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Visit the Official Website<br></strong>Go to the official Bhoomi website: <a href="https://landrecords.karnataka.gov.in" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">landrecords.karnataka.gov.in</a>.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-10_d0e4be-79"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Select Survey Documents Request<br></strong>Scroll down the page and click on <strong>&#8220;Request for Survey Documents&#8221;</strong> under the <strong>Survey (SSLR) Services</strong> section.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-10_717e72-7b"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Enter Registered Number<br></strong>On the new page, enter your <strong>registered number</strong>.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-10_3fce8b-c5"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Verify with OTP<br></strong>An OTP (One-Time Password) will be sent to your registered mobile number. Enter the OTP to verify your identity.</span></li>
